id=\"0\",\n                mkstream=True,\n            )\n        except ResponseError as exc:\n            if \"BUSYGROUP\" not in str(exc):\n                raise\n\n    async def enqueue(self, groupname=self.settings.consumer_group,\n            min=\"-\",\n            max=\"+\",\n            count=count,\n            idle=min_idle_ms,\n        )\n        if not pending:\n            return queue: str) -> int:\n        stream = self._stream(queue)\n        return await self.redis.xlen(stream)\n\n    async def publish_dlq(self, fields: Mapping[str, str]) -> str:\n        return str(await TaskSpec,\n)\n\n\nclass SleepPayload(BaseModel):\n    seconds: float = Field(ge=0.0, le=300.0)\n\n\nclass HttpGetPayload(BaseModel):\n    url: HttpUrl\n    timeout: float = Field(default=5.0, ge=0.1, le=60.0)\n\n\nclass CpuBurnPayload(BaseModel):\n    iterations: int = Field(default=50_000, ge=1, le=5_000_000)\n\n\nclass FailThenSucceedPayload(BaseModel):\n    failures: int = Field(default=1, Field(default=0.2, ge=0.0, le=30.0)\n\n\nasync def task_sleep(ctx: TaskContext, payload: SleepPayload) -> dict[str, Any]:\n    await ctx.checkpoint()\n    if payload.seconds > 0:\n        import asyncio\n\n        await asyncio.sleep(payload.seconds)\n    await ctx.checkpoint()\n    return {\"slept_seconds\": payload.seconds}\n\n\nasync def task_http_get(_: TaskContext, payload: HttpGetPayload) -> dict[str, Any]:\n    try:\n        async with httpx.AsyncClient(timeout=payload.timeout) as client:\n            response = await client.get(str(payload.url))\n    except httpx.HTTPError as exc:\n        raise RetryableTaskError(f\"HTTP request failed: {exc}\") from exc\n\n    if response.status_code >= 500:\n        raise RetryableTaskError(f\"Server error status: {response.status_code}\")\n\n    if response.status_code >= 400:\n        raise FatalTaskError(f\"Client error status: {response.status_code}\")\n\n    body = response.text[:200]\n    return {\n        \"status_code\": response.status_code,\n        \"body_preview\": body,\n        \"url\": str(payload.url),\n    }\n\n\nasync def task_cpu_burn(_: TaskContext, payload: CpuBurnPayload) -> dict[str, Any]:\n    digest = b\"seed\"\n    for i in range(payload.iterations):\n        digest = hashlib.sha256(digest + str(i).encode(\"utf-8\")).digest()\n    return {\"iterations\": payload.iterations, \"digest\": digest.hex()}\n\n\nasync def task_fail_then_succeed(\n    ctx: TaskContext,\n    payload: FailThenSucceedPayload,\n) -> dict[str, Any]:\n    if ctx.attempt <= payload.failures:\n        raise RetryableTaskError(f\"Forced failure for attempt {ctx.attempt}\")\n    return {\"value\": payload.value, \"attempt\": ctx.attempt}\n\n\nasync def task_pipeline_demo(ctx: TaskContext, payload: PipelineDemoPayload) -> dict[str, Any]:\n    import asyncio\n\n    completed: list[str] = []\n    for step in payload.steps:\n        await ctx.checkpoint()\n        if payload.step_delay > 0:\n            await asyncio.sleep(payload.step_delay)\n        completed.append(step)\n    await ctx.checkpoint()\n    return {\"completed_steps\": completed, \"count\": len(completed)}\n\n\ndef import BaseModel, ValidationError\n\nfrom mini_celery.backoff import BackoffPolicy\n\n\nclass TaskExecutionError(Exception):\n    def __init__(self, message: str, retryable: bool):\n  job_id: str\n    attempt: int\n    should_cancel: Callable[[], bool]\n\n    async def checkpoint(self) -> None:\n        if self.should_cancel():\n            raise JobCancelledError()\n        await self.get(task_type).backoff_policy\n\n    def names(self) -> list[str]:\n        return sorted(self._tasks.keys())\n"
